/*
1. Use a consistent sensible line-height in all browsers.
2. Prevent adjustments of font size after orientation changes in iOS.
3. Use a more readable tab size.
4. Use the user's configured `sans` font-family by default.
5. Use the user's configured `sans` font-feature-settings by default.
6. Use the user's configured `sans` font-variation-settings by default.
7. Disable tap highlights on iOS
*/

html,
:host {
  line-height: 1.5; /* 1 */
  -webkit-text-size-adjust: 100%; /* 2 */
  -moz-tab-size: 4; /* 3 */
  -o-tab-size: 4;
     tab-size: 4; /* 3 */
  font-family: ui-sans-serif, system-ui, sans-serif, "Apple Color Emoji", "Segoe UI Emoji", "Segoe UI Symbol", "Noto Color Emoji"; /* 4 */
  font-feature-settings: normal; /* 5 */
  font-variation-settings: normal; /* 6 */
  -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; /* 7 */
}

/*
1. Remove the margin in all browsers.
2. Inherit line-height from `html` so users can set them as a class directly on the `html` element.
*/

  margin: 0; /* 1 */
  line-height: inherit; /* 2 */
}

1. Add the correct height in Firefox.

</div> </div> </div> </article>  <script>
  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });
</script><article class="group relative bg-white rounded-[2rem] overflow-hidden shadow-sm hover:shadow-2xl transition-all duration-500 border border-stone-100/50 flex flex-col" data-cat="dia-madre"   document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });
</script><article class="group relative bg-white rounded-[2rem] overflow-hidden shadow-sm hover:shadow-2xl transition-all duration-500 border border-stone-100/50 flex flex-col" data-cat="dia-madre"   document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

</div> </div> </div> </article>  <script>
  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });
</script> </div> </section> <section class="max-w-[1400px] mx-auto px-4 md:px-6 py-10 md:py-14" data-astro-source-file="C:/Users/jhona/Downloads/nuditos-astro-paso1/src/pages/index.astro" data-astro-source-loc="131:79"> <div class="flex items-center justify-between mb-5 pb-2 border-b border-stone-200" data-astro-source-file="C:/Users/jhona/Downloads/nuditos-astro-paso1/src/pages/index.astro" data-astro-source-loc="132:96"> <h2 class="uppercase font-bold tracking-widest text-[#1a1220] text-xs md:text-sm" data-astro-source-file="C:/Users/jhona/Downloads/nuditos-astro-paso1/src/pages/index.astro" data-astro-source-loc="133:97">Noche estrellada</h2> <a href="/catalogo?categoria=noche-estrellada" class="text-[9px] md:text-[10px] tracking-widest uppercase font-bold text-stone-500 hover:text-stone-900 border border-stone-200 px-3 py-1 bg-white hover:bg-stone-50 transition-colors" data-astro-source-file="C:/Users/jhona/Downloads/nuditos-astro-paso1/src/pages/index.astro" data-astro-source-loc="134:280">

  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init

        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);

              dot.classList.add('w-2');

</div> </div> </div> </article>  <script>
  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });
</script><article class="group relative bg-white rounded-[2rem] overflow-hidden shadow-sm hover:shadow-2xl transition-all duration-500 border border-stone-100/50 flex flex-col" </div> </div> </div> </article>  <script>
  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });
</script><article class="group relative bg-white rounded-[2rem] overflow-hidden shadow-sm hover:shadow-2xl transition-all duration-500 border border-stone-100/50 flex flex-col" data-cat="dia-madre"   document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

</div> </div> </div> </article>  <script>
  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });
</script><article class="group relative bg-white rounded-[2rem] overflow-hidden shadow-sm hover:shadow-2xl transition-all duration-500 border border-stone-100/50 flex flex-col" data-cat="macetas"   document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

</div> </div> </div> </article>  <script>
  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

</div> </div> </div> </article>  <script>
  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {

  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

</div> </div> </div> </article>  <script>
  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });
</script><article class="group relative bg-white rounded-[2rem] overflow-hidden shadow-sm hover:shadow-2xl transition-all duration-500 border border-stone-100/50 flex flex-col" data-cat="rapunzel"   document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

</div> </div> </div> </article>  <script>
  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });

  document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
    // Sincronización de dots para carruseles de tarjetas
    document.querySelectorAll('.snap-x').forEach(container => {
      const dots = container.parentElement.querySelectorAll('[data-idx]');
      if(!dots.length) return;
      
      // Init
      if (dots[0]) {
        dots[0].classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
        dots[0].classList.add('w-2');
      }

      let isScrolling;
      container.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        window.clearTimeout(isScrolling);
        isScrolling = setTimeout(() => {
          const idx = Math.round(container.scrollLeft / container.clientWidth);
          dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
            if(i === idx) {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white/40', 'bg-white');
              dot.classList.add('w-2');
            } else {
              dot.classList.replace('bg-white', 'bg-white/40');
              dot.classList.remove('w-2');
            }
          });
        }, 60);
      }, { passive: true });
    });

    // Controles por botones (Desktop)
    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-prev').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: -target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });

    document.querySelectorAll('.carousel-next').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        const target = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
        if (target) target.scrollBy({ left: target.clientWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
      });
    });
  });
</script> </div> </section>  <div id="filteredView" style="display: none;" class="pb-24 pt-12" data-astro-source-file="C:/Users/jhona/Downloads/nuditos-astro-paso1/src/pages/index.astro"     // Lógica Simple de Active State para Mobile Nav
    function updateActiveNav() {
      const path = window.location.pathname;
      const hash = window.location.hash;
      const navCatalogo = document.getElementById('nav-catalogo');
      const navPersonalizado = document.getElementById('nav-personalizado');

      if (!navCatalogo || !navPersonalizado) return;

      navCatalogo.classList.remove('active');
      navPersonalizado.classList.remove('active');

      if (path.includes('/catalogo')) {
        navCatalogo.classList.add('active');
      } else if (hash === '#personalizado') {
        navPersonalizado.classList.add('active');
      }
    }

    // Lógica de Cabecera Inteligente
    (function() {
      let lastScroll = window.pageYOffset;

      function handleSmartHeader() {
        const nav = document.querySelector('.nav-wrap');
        if (!nav) return;
        
        const currentScroll = window.pageYOffset;

        if (currentScroll <= 15) {
          nav.classList.remove('nav-hidden');
          nav.classList.remove('nav-scrolled');
          lastScroll = currentScroll;
          return;
        }

        nav.classList.add('nav-scrolled');

        if (currentScroll > lastScroll) {
          if (currentScroll > 80) nav.classList.add('nav-hidden');
        } else {
          nav.classList.remove('nav-hidden');
        }
        
        lastScroll = currentScroll;
      }

      document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
        updateActiveNav();
        // Resetear scroll al cambiar de página
        lastScroll = window.pageYOffset;
        window.addEventListener('scroll', handleSmartHeader, { passive: true });
      });
      window.addEventListener('hashchange', updateActiveNav);
    })();
  </script> <!-- ════════ FOOTER ════════ --> <footer data-astro-cid-sckkx6r4 data-astro-source-file="C:/Users/jhona/Downloads/nuditos-astro-paso1/src/layouts/Layout.astro" defer></script> <script src="/scripts/supabase.js" defer></script> <script src="/scripts/emails.js" defer></script> <script src="/scripts/app.js" defer></script>  <!-- Lógica de Swipe Down para el carrito en Mobile --> <script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
      const cartDrag = document.getElementById('cartHeaderDrag');
      const cartPanel = document.getElementById('cartPanel');
      if (!cartDrag || !cartPanel) return;

      let startY = 0;
      let currentY = 0;
      let isDragging = false;

      cartDrag.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => {
        if (window.innerWidth >= 768) return; // Solo móvil
        startY = e.touches[0].clientY;
        isDragging = true;
        cartPanel.style.transition = 'none'; // Quitar transición durante arrastre
      }, {passive: true});

      cartDrag.addEventListener('touchmove', (e) => {
        if (!isDragging) return;
        currentY = Math.max(0, e.touches[0].clientY - startY); // Solo arrastre hacia abajo
        cartPanel.style.transform = `translateY(${currentY}px)`;
        e.preventDefault();
      }, {passive: false});

      cartDrag.addEventListener('touchend', () => {
        if (!isDragging) return;
        isDragging = false;
        cartPanel.style.transition = ''; // Restaurar transición CSS

        if (currentY > 80) { // Umbral para cerrar
          // Resetear translateY y cerrar normalmente
          cartPanel.style.transform = ''; 
          if(typeof toggleCart === 'function') toggleCart();
        } else {
          // Rebotar a posición original
          cartPanel.style.transform = '';
        }
        currentY = 0;
      });
    });
  </script> <!-- Slot para scripts extra de cada página -->  <script>(function(){const liveConfig = {"descuentoActivo":false,"descuentoCodigo":"NUDITOS10","descuentoPorcentaje":10,"descuentoTexto":"10% de descuento en tu primer pedido","carruselHero":[71,18,1,2,10,6,78,72],"ramoDestacado":74,"wompiActivo":true,"wompiKey":"pub_test_v8JHkR70Tk6ApnLxbz2w0pRqDVFbwgZ1","wompiIntegrity":"test_integrity_EgEP2HBhfJP1Si10xqsy6B5qVyVRcXij","wompiEvents":"test_events_KsjFESHfSPg12ZLa4Nw4KbEKMcnw8nl0","catViews":{},"seleccionNuditos":[132,130,129,131],"metaPixelActivo":false,"metaPixelId":"","seoTitle":"","seoDescription":"","seoOgImage":"","socialInstagram":"","socialWhatsapp":"","gaId":"","gaActive":false};

    document.addEventListener('astro:page-load', () => {
      const videos = document.querySelectorAll('video[autoplay][muted]');
      videos.forEach(v => {
        v.play().catch(() => {
          // Si falla, intentamos de nuevo al primer toque del usuario

            v.play();

          document.addEventListener('click', forcePlay);
          document.addEventListener('touchstart', forcePlay);
